  <script>
  
  // Function to calculate the total price from repeater fields
  function calculateTotalPrice() {
    let totalPrice = 0;

    // Get all the price input fields
    const priceInputs = document.querySelectorAll('.price input');

    // Loop through each price input field
    priceInputs.forEach((priceInput) => {
      // If the input has a valid value, add it to the total price
      if (priceInput.value !== '') {
        totalPrice += parseFloat(priceInput.value);
      }
    });

    // Update the input field with the total price
    // const totalInput = document.getElementById('nf-field-1118');
	const hiddentotalInput = document.getElementById('nf-field-1122');
	
	const totalInput = jQuery('#nf-field-1118');
	
    if (totalInput) {      
	   totalInput.val(totalPrice.toFixed(2)).trigger('change');	  
    }
  }

  // Call the calculateTotalPrice function when the page is ready
  document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', calculateTotalPrice);

  // Attach an event listener to the price input fields and "Add Item" button to recalculate the total when values change
  document.addEventListener('input', calculateTotalPrice);
  const addItemButton = document.querySelector('.nf-add-fieldset');
  if (addItemButton) {
    addItemButton.addEventListener('click', calculateTotalPrice);
  }

  // Add event delegation for the "Remove Fieldset" buttons
  document.addEventListener('click', (event) => {
    const removeButton = event.target.closest('.nf-remove-fieldset');
    if (removeButton) {
      calculateTotalPrice();
    }
  });
</script>

<div class="flex_column av-1126n6h-ea58d941a19e2ce4656e7f5431b1e26f av_one_fifth  avia-builder-el-9  el_after_av_submenu  el_before_av_three_fifth  avia-builder-el-first  first flex_column_div av-zero-column-padding "></div>
<div class="flex_column av-kvi3zvd-1ffcc6abdc2bb37a09590f68cdb84a0d av_three_fifth  avia-builder-el-10  el_after_av_one_fifth  el_before_av_one_full  flex_column_div av-zero-column-padding "><div class="av-special-heading av-kc8x08p-caa1c4309fb9ba1340680358ebf9d30a av-special-heading-h1 custom-color-heading blockquote modern-quote modern-centered  avia-builder-el-11  el_before_av_textblock  avia-builder-el-first "><h1 class="av-special-heading-tag" itemprop="headline">Explore Hillary’s Hut Through Virtual Reality</h1><div class="special-heading-border"><div class="special-heading-inner-border"></div></div></div>
<section class="av_textblock_section av-jvm37zt-a45d317496f2e6b8c368b83fa2116ca3" itemscope="itemscope" itemtype="https://schema.org/CreativeWork"><div class="avia_textblock av_inherit_color" itemprop="text"><p>Antarctic Heritage Trust invites you to explore Sir Edmund Hillary’s Antarctic hut through a new, ground-breaking virtual reality experience.</p>
<p>In partnership with Auckland University of Technology (AUT) the Trust has developed this virtual reality experience to celebrate New Zealand’s first presence in Antarctica.</p>
</div></section></div>
<div class="flex_column av-r9b0xl-5ce80553382c9c170a8566135dc5a313 av_one_full  avia-builder-el-13  el_after_av_three_fifth  el_before_av_layout_row  avia-builder-el-last  first flex_column_div av-zero-column-padding "></div>
</div></div></div><!-- close content main div --></div></div><div id="av-layout-grid-2" class="av-layout-grid-container av-ra516h-ab7d0843faa20b9b0c4aaadcc0c00b8e entry-content-wrapper main_color av-flex-cells  avia-builder-el-14  el_after_av_one_full  el_before_av_one_full  grid-row-not-first  container_wrap fullsize">
<div class="flex_cell av_one_half av-l327s52h-fcea1a65874ffd7d94719764b612a470 no_margin  avia-builder-el-15  el_before_av_cell_one_half  avia-builder-el-first "><div class="flex_cell_inner">
<section class="av_textblock_section av-ifosjyx-90e0caaa0413446f6f9156aa0b5bdf29" itemscope="itemscope" itemtype="https://schema.org/CreativeWork"><div class="avia_textblock" itemprop="text"><h2>Book VR for my School or Community Group</h2>
<p>Antarctic Heritage Trust is touring Hillary’s Hut – Antarctica Virtual Reality Experience around schools and community groups and events in New Zealand. If you would like the team to bring the experience to your school, community group or event fill in the form and someone will be in touch soon. Thank you to our national tour sponsor <a href="https://www.dulux.co.nz/about-us/partnerships/antarctic-heritage-trust/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Dulux New Zealand</a>.</p>
</div></section>
<div class="hr av-ibcszh5-e321a6205ffac362f205e2c06fb12f02 hr-invisible  avia-builder-el-17  el_after_av_textblock  el_before_av_textblock "><span class="hr-inner "><span class="hr-inner-style"></span></span></div>

<p>To view the virtual experience on your mobile device, visit the App Store or Google Play and download it for free (view in VR with your cardboard headset).</p>
</div></section></div><div class="flex_column av-xtdeah-76aef2c6d889ed52d8af6a23395bf928 av_one_half  avia-builder-el-33  el_after_av_one_half  el_before_av_one_fourth  flex_column_div av-zero-column-padding column-top-margin"><section class="av_textblock_section av-93iuz15-685902548721cab3b4dd7d222b55f400" itemscope="itemscope" itemtype="https://schema.org/CreativeWork"><div class="avia_textblock" itemprop="text"><h2><span style="color: #000000;">Experience the fully immersive version</span></h2>
<p>To experience the fully immersive version, download it for free from Steam and watch it on your HTC Vive headset or access the updated Hillary’s Hut – Antarctica experience from Vive Focus 3 from the VIVE Business App Store.</p>

<div class="flex_column av-83xhuvt-fac67e115d4b2c674dae26872113247c av_three_fifth  avia-builder-el-44  el_after_av_hr  el_before_av_two_fifth  first flex_column_div av-zero-column-padding "><section class="av_textblock_section av-7jl8tyx-77932abbcd016de4e721ee2c8c209b3a" itemscope="itemscope" itemtype="https://schema.org/CreativeWork"><div class="avia_textblock" itemprop="text"><h2>Step Inside</h2>
</div></section>
<section class="av_textblock_section av-6ye19ll-1f7da9779c91c5be9ff0f16c9fc20027" itemscope="itemscope" itemtype="https://schema.org/CreativeWork"><div class="avia_textblock" itemprop="text"><p>Antarctic Heritage Trust is a world leader in cold-climate heritage conservation and in 2017 completed the conservation of the first 1957 building erected at New Zealand’s Scott Base in Antarctica.</p>
<p>Antarctic Heritage Trust invites you to explore Sir Edmund Hillary’s Antarctic hut through a new, ground-breaking virtual reality experience.<br>
In partnership with Auckland University of Technology (AUT) and Staples VR the Trust has developed this virtual reality experience to celebrate New Zealand’s connection with Antarctica.</p>
<p>This large scale project brings Antarctica to people in a way never seen before.</p>
<p>Hillary’s Hut was initially used as a base for the party of 23 men engaged in exploration and important scientific research as part of the Commonwealth Trans-Antarctic Expedition (TAE) and the New Zealand party of the International Geophysical Year (IGY).</p>
<p>Join us and step inside Sir Ed’s Antarctic hut and find out what life was like living in the world’s most extreme environment as these men furthered science and exploration.</p>
<p>Thanks to Antarctica New Zealand for their support.</p>
</div></section>
<div class="hr av-6iehj3t-f870607b35694d74200e240d00cbba86 hr-invisible  avia-builder-el-47  el_after_av_textblock  el_before_av_textblock "><span class="hr-inner "><span class="hr-inner-style"></span></span></div>
<section class="av_textblock_section av-22cvemx-3f95ba542ec89b893df4d336cd08b1f1" itemscope="itemscope" itemtype="https://schema.org/CreativeWork"><div class="avia_textblock" itemprop="text"><h2>Education Resources</h2>
<p>Download Hillary’s Hut Virtual Reality brochure <a href="https://nzaht.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/Vr-Brochure-720x594mm_LowRes.pdf">here</a>.</p>
<p>Learn more about the exploration undertaken as part of the Trans-Antarctic Expedition (TAE) and the science done as part of the International Geophysical Year (IGY).</p>
</div></section>

<section class="av_textblock_section av-11kism1-b307429c6f595b4d1191ad08a3f7c67f" itemscope="itemscope" itemtype="https://schema.org/CreativeWork"><div class="avia_textblock" itemprop="text"><h2>Help us make more experiences like this one</h2>
<p>The Trust is excited to keep making virtual reality experiences. You can help us make more experiences like Hillary’s Hut – Antarctica by making a <a href="https://nzaht.org/sustain/support-our-work/donate/">donation here.</a></p>

function myFunction() {
  var x = document.getElementById("flinks");
  var up = document.getElementById("icon_up");
  var down = document.getElementById("icon_down");
  if (x.style.display === "flex") {
    x.style.display = "none";
  } else {
    x.style.display = "flex";
  }

  if (up.style.display === "inline") {
    up.style.display = "none";
    down.style.display = "inline";
  } else {
    up.style.display = "inline";
    down.style.display = "none";
  }

}
